rus\"></span>\n\t\t\t</p>\n\t\t\t<p class=\"pg-card-description desc\">\n\t\t\t\tThe most prominent hackers used the alias Guccifer 2.0. U.S. intelligence officials believe Guccifer 2.0 is a Russian military agent or a persona that was used by multiple people to publicize hacked materials. Analysts are skeptical Guccifer 2.0 conducted the actual hacking, but agree with officials that the name was used as a front to disclose materials online. Hackers with two Russian spy agencies penetrated the systems of the Democratic National Committee and the accounts of other political party members and organizations. They are the FSB, or Federal Security Service, a successor to the KGB; and the GRU, Russia&#39;s military intelligence organization. Guccifer 2.0 was a persona --or the online moniker--affiliated with the release of information hacked by the GRU. class=\"pg-card-title\">\n\t\t\t\tRussian hackers <span class=\"flag rus\"></span>\n\t\t\t</p>\n\t\t\t<p class=\"pg-card-description desc\">\n\t\t\t\tThe most prominent hackers used the alias Guccifer 2.0. U.S. intelligence officials believe Guccifer 2.0 is a Russian military agent or a persona that was used by multiple people to publicize hacked materials. Analysts are skeptical Guccifer 2.0 conducted the actual hacking, but agree with officials that the name was used as a front to disclose materials online. Hackers with two Russian spy agencies penetrated the systems of the Democratic National Committee and the accounts of other political party members and organizations. They are the FSB, or Federal Security Service, a successor to the KGB; and the GRU, Russia&#39;s military intelligence organization. Guccifer 2.0 was a persona --or the online moniker--affiliated with the release of information hacked by the GRU. Analysts are skeptical that Guccifer 2.0 conducted the actual hacking, but agree with officials that the name was used as a front to disclose materials online.\n\t\t\t</p>\n\t\t</div>\n\n\n\n\t\t<div class=\"connex-wrap cf pg-card-margin--sides pg-card-margin--bottom\">\n\t\t\t<p class=\"smallhed\">Ties to Team Trump</p>\n\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\n<a href=\"#\" data-slug=\"stone\">\n\t<div class=\"connect\">\n\t\t<p>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\tStone\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</p>\n\t\t\n\t\t\t<img src=\"img/people/stone.jpg\">\n\t\t\n\t</div>\n</a>\n\n\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\n\n\t\t\t\n\t\t</div>\n\n\n\n\t\t\n\n\t</div>\n\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\n\t\t\n\t\t\n\t\t\t<div class=\"col-md-4 col-sm-8 card-container\">\n\t\t\t\n\n\t\n\n\t<div class=\"pg-card card \" data-slug=\"gorkov\" id=\"gorkov\">\n\n\t\t<div class=\"head-wrap pg-card-margin--top pg-card-margin--bottom pg-card-margin--sides cf\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"mug\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t<img src=\"img/people/generic-male.jpg\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t<p class=\"pg-card-title\">\n\t\t\t\tSergey N.
